###  Paristo‚ÇÅ

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Paristo* (battery)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  1
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  LAST
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
